0                                   1941      13.              COPY  SLISTMAC
                                    1942             =*******************************************************************
                                    1943             =*                                                                 *
                                    1944             =* Macros for the serialized manipulation of single linked lists   *
                                    1945             =* in memory.  These lists are of the PUSH/POP (LIFO) variety.     *
                                    1946             =* Serialization is achieved using the CDS and CS instructions.    *
                                    1947             =*                                                                 *
                                    1948             =*******************************************************************
0                                   1950             =*******************************************************************
                                    1951             =*                                                                 *
                                    1952             =* Single linked list head fields                                  *
                                    1953             =*                                                                 *
                                    1954             =*******************************************************************
                                    1955             =         MACRO
                                    1956             =&LAB     SHEAD
                                    1957             =         AIF   ('&LAB' EQ '').ERR
                                    1958             =&LAB     DS   0D                   Single linked CDS list
                                    1959             =&LAB.FP  DS    A                   Forward pointer
                                    1960             =&LAB.SEQ DS    A                   CDS sequence number
                                    1961             =         MEXIT
                                    1962             =.ERR     MNOTE 8,'Label (list name) required'
                                    1963             =         MEND
0                                   1965             =*******************************************************************
                                    1966             =*                                                                 *
                                    1967             =* Push an item onto a single linked list                          *
                                    1968             =*                                                                 *
                                    1969             =*******************************************************************
                                    1970             =         MACRO
                                    1971             =&LABEL   SPUSH &HEAD=,&ITEM=
                                    1972             =         LCLC  &X
                                    1973             =         AIF   ('&LABEL' EQ '').NOLAB
                                    1974             =&LABEL   LABEL ,
                                    1975             =.NOLAB   ANOP  ,
                                    1976             =         AIF   ('&HEAD' EQ '').ERR1
                                    1977             =         AIF   ('&ITEM' EQ '').ERR2
                                    1979             =         LM    R14,R15,&HEAD       Get fwd ptr and sequence number
                                    1980             =         LA    RVR,&ITEM           Point to new item
                                    1981             =         LOOP  BEGIN
                                    1982             =         LA    RS,1(R15)           Increment sequence
                                    1983             =         MVC   &ITEM.(L'&HEAD.FP),&HEAD.FP Set item fwd ptr
                                    1984             =         CDS   R14,RVR,&HEAD       Add item to list
                                    1985             =         UNTIL (Z),END
                                    1987             =         AGO   .EXIT
                                    1988             =.ERR1    MNOTE 8,'Head is a required parameter'
                                    1989             =         AGO   .EXIT
                                    1990             =.ERR2    MNOTE 8,'Item is a required parameter'
                                    1991             =.EXIT    ANOP  ,
                                    1992             =         MEND  ,

 000016                00000 03048  4403      88.     FILECAT  CSECT ,
                                    4405      89.     *---------------------------------------------------------------------*
                                    4406      90.     *  FILECAT - File system catalog manager
                                    4407      91.     *
                                    4408      92.     *   This module handles all catalog processing requests. It is part
                                    4409      93.     *   of the file system rewrite. The actual catalog access is still
                                    4410      94.     *   done in VCAT which is a module from the old file system. VCAT is
                                    4411      95.     *   not being rewritten at this time. The interface to VCAT is done
                                    4412      96.     *   with many registers and a dummy RQBL which is the file request
                                    4413      97.     *   block from the old file system. VCAT is also used in the offline
                                    4414      98.     *   catalog rebuild process. It is not being rewritten because of the
                                    4415      99.     *   size of the task, especially verifying it still works the same both
                                    4416     100.     *   online and offline.
                                    4417     101.     *
                                    4418     102.     *---------------------------------------------------------------------*
